d) This will be understood through a parable from the *Seder Hishtalshelus* in the human soul: the garments of the soul—thought, speech, and action—whose root is from the *midos*, and the *midos* whose root is from the intellect, and the intellect whose root is from the power of the *maskil* (the intellect-possessor). All these levels belong to one another. The matter is that thought, speech, and action, whose root is in the *midos*, are in a way that there is an inclusion of the thought, speech, and action in the *midos*. For thought, speech, and action are the garments of the soul, like a garment through which the one clothed in it is revealed—that is, the thought, speech, and action reveal the *midos*. Thus, the power of revelation in the *midos* is the matter of the inclusion of thought, speech, and action in the *midos*. Likewise, there is the matter of the *midos* in thought, speech, and action, as the *midos* give vitality to the thought, speech, and action. Similarly, in the *midos* whose root is from the intellect, there is an inclusion of the *midos* in the intellect, which is the matter of the *hispaalus* of the intellect (for *hispaalus* is a different essence than intellect, and it is the matter of the inclusion of the *midos* in the intellect). Likewise, there is the matter of the intellect in the *midos*, as the intellect effects vitality and growth in the *midos*. Similarly, in the intellect whose root is from the power of the *maskil*, even though the revelation of the intellect comes specifically through exertion—which indicates that the power of the *maskil* is not an intellect-existence, and the invention of the intellect from it is like *yesh me'ayin*—nevertheless, since through exertion an intellect is found from it, and nothing but intellect is found from it, it is a source for the intellect. This is the matter of the inclusion of the intellect in the power of the *maskil*. Likewise, there is the matter of the power of the *maskil* in the intellect, as there are matters of the intellect that do not come into understanding and explanation, as in "a great scholar... but he does not return to it," which is from the side of the revelation of the power of the *maskil*. That is, it is not as it remains in concealment in the power of the *maskil*, but as it comes into revelation, only that it is not the revelation of the intellect, but the revelation of the power of the *maskil*. From this, it is understood that there is a connection and belonging between all the details of the levels in the aforementioned *Seder Hishtalshelus*, from the power of the *maskil* to thought, speech, and action.

However, in order for there to be an extension of the powers from the essence of the soul, which is simple in the ultimate sense, this is not by way of *Hishtalshelus*, but by way of *yesh me'ayin*. Its parallel above is that all the details of the levels in the *Seder Hishtalshelus* have value and connection to one another, but they have no value at all regarding the *Ohr Ein Sof* the Emanator, because it is *Ohr Ein Sof* that does not give place for the standing of the worlds, as it is in *Etz Chaim* that at first the *Ohr Ein Sof* filled the void and there was no place for the standing of the worlds, and afterwards He removed His great light to the side and extended a short and thin *Kav*. From this, it is understood that there is no value or connection for the worlds with the *Ohr Ein Sof* the Emanator, for for the coming-into-being of the worlds, there had to be a *Tzimtzum* in the manner of the removal of the light, etc., because it is *Ohr Ein Sof* that is completely above the worlds. That is, the coming-into-being of the worlds from the *Ohr Ein Sof* the Emanator is not by way of *Hishtalshelus*, but by way of *yesh me'ayin*.

e) Now, even though the level of *Ohr Ein Sof* before the *Tzimtzum* is above connection to the worlds, as it does not give place for the worlds, nevertheless, there is extended from it into the worlds as they are after the *Tzimtzum* (not only the light of the *Kav* that was clothed in the *Tzimtzum*, but) also from the level of the great circle over which the *Tzimtzum* has no control (even though the *Tzimtzum* touched it). However, in order for its extension to be in the world, it comes through the passage of the *Tzimtzum*, but only by way of a conduit, so it does not change from its essence, and therefore it is in the category of *Ein Sof* like the *Ohr Ein Sof* before the *Tzimtzum*. As is known, this is one of the explanations regarding the *Hishtalshelus* of the crowns from one another, that even the circles after the *Tzimtzum*, even though they are extended from the *Kav* (as it is in *Etz Chaim* that the *Kav* extends and circles, etc.), nevertheless, they are connected with the level of the great circle before the *Tzimtzum*, which is what is extended only through the conduit of the *Tzimtzum*. This is also the general difference between circles and *yosher* (straight): *yosher* is the light that was clothed in the *Tzimtzum* and its essence changed and it came into division, etc., and circles is the light that came through the conduit of the *Tzimtzum* and its essence did not change, which is why even below it is in the category of *Ein Sof* that is above division.

The parable for this in created beings below is the difference between earth and water. Earth has division, as it is in *Avos D'Rabbi Nosson* that the earth has a head, body, and feet, like the division in a person, where the general vitality in the head is divided into three parts, which are the three *mochin* *Chabad* that are clothed in the three cavities of the brain that are divided from one another. From these three *mochin* branch out the three senses of sight, hearing, and speech (the sense of sight from *Chochma*, the sense of hearing from *Binah*, and the sense of speech from *Daas*, as it is written, "From His mouth is *Daas*." Therefore, the angels are called by the names of beast, lion, and ox, etc., for they do not have *Daas* (that is, *Daas* of the Above, but only *Daas* of the below) and they do not have speech. This is what is said, "After the *Havayah* they shall walk, like a lion he shall roar," which refers to the camp of Michael, the level of the face of the lion to the right—that is, he does not have actual speech like a person who speaks with *Daas*, but rather he roars with a voice without speech). And when they extend further below, they come into the three parts of the trachea, esophagus, and veins in the neck, which is the intermediary that connects the head and the body. And afterwards, in the descent of the powers below into the body, they are divided into right hand, left hand, and the body, and further below, right foot, left foot, and the body. Likewise, there is also in the earth all the details of division that there are in a person.

Water, however, does not have division. Even though there is the distinction between upper waters and lower waters, as it is written, "And He divided between the waters, etc.," it is all one essence of water. Moreover, even the creatures in the water that are divided from one another in their image, likeness, character, and form, are equal in that their existence is the existence of water, which is why when they are separated from the water, they immediately die. The reason for the difference between earth and water is because the earth's root is from the level of *yosher*, and therefore it has division, and water's root is from the level of circles, which even in their descent below, their essence did not change. Therefore, even in created beings whose root is from the level of circles, there is this matter that they are one essence that is above division.

f) However, even in the level of circles that were extended from the level of the great circle only through the conduit of the *Tzimtzum* (which is why their essence did not change and they are in the category of *Ein Sof*), since they were extended through the conduit of the *Tzimtzum* at all, they also have from the level of the *Tzimtzum*. It can be said that there are two levels in the circles. The first level in it is the dominance of the level of *Ein Sof*, and the second level in it is the dominance of the level of the *Tzimtzum*. This is the difference between upper waters and lower waters, for water in general is the level of circles (as above), only that upper waters is the higher level in the circles in which there is the dominance of the level of *Ein Sof*, and lower waters is the lower level in the circles, in which there is the dominance of the level of the *Tzimtzum*.

In general, the level of lower waters, the lower level in the circles, is the level of the angels, who are called *nuni yama* (fish of the sea), for they are like fish in the sea, which is the level of circles (as above, that the root of water is from the level of circles), only that they are the lower level in the circles (lower waters) in which there is the dominance of the level of the *Tzimtzum*. Similarly in the angels, their existence is in dominance, unlike in the *Sefiros* where there is the dominance of the level of *Ein Sof*. For even though the *Sefiros* were also touched by the *Tzimtzum* to be in the number of ten specifically—ten and not nine, ten and not eleven—their existence is *Elokus*. Not only in the world of *Atzilus*, where "He and His life are one, He and His causes are one," but even as they are in *Beriah*, where it is not "one with them," their existence is *Elokus* (and only the palaces that come into being from *ayin* to *yesh* are in the category of *yesh* and existence). That is, in the *Sefiros* there is the dominance of the level of *Ein Sof*, as the existence of the *Sefiros* is the light that is clothed within them.

Unlike the angels, who, despite being in total *bitul* to *Elokus*, to the point that we find that the angel says about himself, "By Me I have sworn," nevertheless, they are an existence, as it is written, "Thousands of thousands would serve Him, and myriads of myriads would stand before Him," and as it is in the *Zohar*, "The camp of Michael is 180,000 camps, like the number of the banner of Judah, and the camp of Gabriel is 157,000 camps, like the number of the banner of Dan, etc." Chazal said, "Thousands of thousands would serve Him—the number of one battalion, and for His battalions there is no number." Every angel is one of the multitude of angels in every battalion, which is his existence, and his existence is like something that is separated and detached from its source. When coming below into this world, he becomes completely separated, as is known the difference between angels and souls: souls, their essence is *Elokus*, and this is what is said, "The *neshamah* that You have given in me is pure, etc.," that even in its descent below, its essence is the *dveikus* in *Elokus*, only that it is in a way of hidden *dveikus*. We even find in the high souls that even when they are below, their entire existence is *Elokus*, as they said, "I am merely a sign," and the like. Unlike angels, who are an existence, only that at the time the angel fulfills his mission, he is in total *bitul* to the point that he says, "By Me I have sworn," because his existence does not conceal the *Elokus*. This is all the more so regarding the matter of the mitzvos, that even though they are clothed in physical things, nevertheless, from the side of the clothing of the mitzvah, there is no concealment of the face in them. Likewise in the angels, that even though they are an existence, nevertheless, from the side of the fulfillment of the mission, their existence does not conceal *Elokus*. But from their own side, they are an existence, which is from the side of the dominance of the level of the *Tzimtzum* in the lower level in the circles, as above.

g) But to come to the level of *Ohr Ein Sof* that was not touched by the *Tzimtzum*—which is the *Ohr Ein Sof* before the ascent of the desire (for the *Tzimtzum* was in the level of the ascent of the desire, and did not touch the *Ohr Ein Sof* before the ascent of the desire), the level of the Owner of the Will—this is effected through the descent of the soul below to be clothed in the animal soul to clarify and refine it, etc.

The explanation of the matter is that there are two modes of *avodah*: the *avodah* of the divine soul from its own side, and its *avodah* in the clarification of the animal soul. The difference between them is that the *avodah* of the divine soul from its own side is primarily *avodah* based on reason and intellect, and its *avodah* in the clarification of the animal soul is the matter of *mesiras nefesh* that is above reason and intellect. For in the divine soul from its own side, the matter of *mesiras nefesh* in its truth does not apply, for *mesiras nefesh* is the surrender of the desire, while the divine soul's desire is in *Elokus*, and even at the time of sin, it was in faith with Him. Therefore, even when it is in the standing and state of "from the straits I called, etc.," it is only a strait from the outside, from the side of the animal soul, and it is not the strait of the divine soul itself, because from its own side it is attached to *Elokus*. As explained above, the difference between angels and souls is that angels are in the category of existence, unlike souls whose essence is *dveikus* in *Elokus*. The reason for this is because the angels' root is from the level of speech, as it is written, "And by the spirit of His mouth all their host," and therefore they are in the category of existence (and they have matter and form, etc.), unlike souls whose root is from the level of thought, and therefore they are not in the category of existence, but in *dveikus* in *Elokus*. Therefore, even in their clothing in the animal soul, their desire is *Elokus*, and consequently, the truth of the matter of *mesiras nefesh* does not apply to them.

Rather, the divine soul effects the matter of *mesiras nefesh* in the animal soul. The animal soul is lower than the angels, for its desire is specifically in physicality, which is the opposite of *Elokus* (for anything that is not holiness is *Sitra Achra*). When the divine soul acts in the animal soul to turn it into holiness, this is the matter of *mesiras nefesh*. In this itself, the essence of *mesiras nefesh* is not in a way that from the side of the divine soul's comprehension, the elevation of holiness is also felt in the animal soul (for this is only what the divine soul forces upon the animal soul regarding matters of holiness, but the animal soul itself remains in its *yeshus*, etc.), but rather that while it is in its standing and state where it does not belong to the feeling of holiness (*zi veist nit un filt nit vos kedusha iz*), a strait is created for it that its matters, which are the opposite of holiness, are not good for it, etc. Since this matter is the opposite of the nature of the animal soul, this is the truth of the matter of *mesiras nefesh* that it is turned into holiness. When the divine soul effects the matter of *mesiras nefesh* in the animal soul, an elevation is created in the divine soul itself, as the matter of *mesiras nefesh* is renewed within it. For since through the "Power that is wondrous to act," the divine soul is clothed in the animal soul and unites with it, the strait of the animal soul becomes also its (the divine soul's) strait. That is, it is not a strait from the outside, but its own strait, and therefore through this, the matter of *mesiras nefesh* is renewed within it.

Now, this *avodah* (that the divine soul effects the matter of *mesiras nefesh* in the animal soul, and through this, the matter of *mesiras nefesh* is also created within it) reaches the root of the divine soul as it is rooted in the *Atzmus* specifically. The matter is that it is known that the divine soul is from the world of *Tikkun*, and the animal soul is from the world of *Tohu* that preceded *Tikkun*. Therefore, the power of the divine soul to clarify the animal soul is (not from the level of revelations, where *Tohu* preceded *Tikkun*, but) from the side of the *Atzmus* specifically. That is, not only from the level above *Tohu*, where *Tohu* and *Tikkun* are equal, but from the level in which it is said, "And I loved Jacob" specifically, which is as the divine soul is rooted in the *Atzmus*, as the statement, "With whom did He consult? With the souls (and there is a version: with the spirits) of the righteous." The matter of consultation is at a level above the desire. Since He consulted with the souls of the righteous, it follows that the souls of Israel are above even the level of the absolute desire, and through them is the decision of the desire.

For the absolute desire from above is not similar to the absolute desire in a person below, like the desire for a house that exists in the nature of his birth, for "anyone who does not have a house is not a person." Even though the reason for this is because it is so above, that "the glory of man is to dwell in a house," which is what the *Ribono shel Olam* desired, to have for Himself a dwelling place in the lower worlds, and therefore this nature exists also in created beings, nevertheless, above, all matters are specifically by choice. So it is also in the absolute desire, and the decision of the desire is specifically through the souls of Israel, because they are rooted above the level of the desire—in the level of the Owner of the Will. In this level reaches the *avodah* of the clarification of the animal soul, because from this level is extended the power for this *avodah*, and in this level is the intent and desire for the general *avodah* of the clarification of the animal soul.

The matter is that regarding the general matter of *avodah*, we find contradictions in the statements of Chazal. Sometimes it is said that when the Jewish people do the will of the Place, they add strength and power, as it is said, "And now, let the power of the *Havayah* be great." And conversely, G-d forbid, when they do not do the will of the Place, they weaken the power of the Above, as it is said, "The Rock who begot you, you weakened"—that is, the *avodah* is a need of the High. And sometimes it is said, "And what does it matter to the *Ribono shel Olam*... the mitzvos were not given but to refine the creatures with them." It is explained that what Chazal said, "What does it matter to Him, etc.," refers to the "Single Master, Root of all roots," which is the level of the *Atzmus* of *Ohr Ein Sof* before the ascent of the desire, to whom it does not matter at all. Only in the level of *Elokus* that is clothed in the worlds does the matter of *avodah* matter. However, from the fact that they said, "What does it matter to Him, etc. (and nevertheless) the mitzvos were given to refine the creatures with them," it is understood that even in the level of the "Single Master, Root of all roots," that which it does not matter to Him is only the matter of *avodah* from its own side (the *avodah* of the divine soul from its own side), but the refining of the creatures through the *avodah* (the clarification of the animal soul) matters above. The reason for this is because such was the pure desire and the holy will to have the refining of the creatures specifically. From this, it is understood that the *avodah* of the clarification of the animal soul, which is the matter of the refining of the creatures, reaches the level of the *Atzmus* of *Ohr Ein Sof* that is before the ascent of the desire, the Owner of the Will.

h) Based on this, one can explain the matter of the three crowns, that in addition to the two crowns that He placed on the heads of His children, which are the two crowns corresponding to *naaseh* and *nishma*, there is also the third crown that the King took and placed on His head, which corresponds to the matter of the preceding of *naaseh* to *nishma* (as above, section 2). The matter is that the preceding of *naaseh* to *nishma* is the matter of *bitul* to the Owner of the Will specifically, where the *avodah* of *mesiras nefesh* of the clarification of the animal soul reaches, which is with the power of the *Atzmus* where the souls of Israel are rooted (as above, section 7). From this, it is understood that the third crown also belongs to the Jewish people, since it is effected through the *avodah* of the Jewish people, who preceded *naaseh* to *nishma*. Even though in the *Midrash* they said, "The supernal beings crown, etc.," which refers to the angels, this itself depends specifically on the Jewish people, as Chazal said, "The ministering angels do not say song above until the Jewish

---
